VIII. Public Hearings 
8:51 AM - 6:00 PM Public Hearing- National Grid Special Permit  
Public Hearing Opened at 6:17 PM; Greg Bergman from planning gave 
overview of special permit, explaining the demolition and reconstruction and 
upgrade of the Facility. 
No Public Comment; Closed at 6:21 PM; Held open for written comment till 
May 30th at 4:30 PM. 
 
8:53 AM - 6:00 PM Public Hearing Acquisition 111 East Main  
Councilman Kern moved to Cancel public hearing seconded by 
Councilwoman Merrifield, Motion carried. 
 
8:59 AM - 6:05 PM Public Hearing Acquisition 127 East Main St.  
Public Hearing Opened at 6:23 PM, Frank Isler, Esq, Gave overview of 
acquisition of site and condemnation of leasehold Interest on ground floor 
rental unit. Dawn Thomas from Community Development further explained 
the Urban Renewal Plan for the creation of a town square after many public 
meetings and interests in the design.  
Public Comments: 
John McAuliff concerned that the height of proposed new construction would 
be undesirable. 
Laura Jens Smith was concerned about a master developer being appointed 
absent a qualified and eligible hearing, and alluded to campaign donations 
influencing the decisions of the board.  
 
IX. Comments on Resolutions 
John McAuliff on resolution 459-460, against any approvals for Scotts Point in 
Calverton

XI. Open Comments from the Public 
Laura Jens Smith representing Jamesport Greater Civic Association encouraged the 
Town to invest in a Hamlet study of the Jamesport hamlet. Presented a letter to be 
distributed into the record. 
John McAuliff questioned why the public hearing for the imminent domain was not 
held open for written comment. 
  
For more information visit our website at www.townofriverheadny.gov  
 
Kevin Shea spoke of the satellite earth station proposed for Calverton was started 
before approvals and building permits. 
Ron Harari via Zoom quoted a media outlets report of campaign contributions during 
the last cycle, and alluded that it may have influenced the boards decisions. 
Supervisor Hubbard responded that everything is public knowledge and can be 
found on the NYS campaign website.  
Colleen O'Brien via Zoom- questioned the public funds used to supplement the Rink 
in Calverton. Councilman Rothwell reiterated that the Rink was funded entirely 
through private funding and gifted to the Town with contract to assist in a portion of 
the electrical costs.  
XII. Adjournment 
The meeting was closed at 8:05 PM 
 
 
 
 
James Wooten, Town Clerk 
 
NOTICE OF MEETING FOR RIVERHEAD TOWN BOARD & RIVERHEAD TOWN 
COMMUNITY DEVELOPMENT AGENCY  
 
PLEASE TAKE NOTICE that the Town Board Meeting and Riverhead Community 
Development Agency, New York (the “CDA”) meeting scheduled for May 21, 2025 at 6:00 
p.m. at Riverhead Town Hall, 4 W Second St, Riverhead, New York shall proceed as scheduled.     
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE, that in addition to in person attendance, the 
public can watch the May 21, 2025 meetings of the Town Board & CDA via the following 
methods:  
1. Live stream; namely, by viewing it on your television on Channel 22;  
2. Logging on the Town of Riverhead website, www.townofriverheadny.gov and 
clicking on the link “Channel 22” on Quick Links on the home page or by connecting to 
the URL, which is as follows: townofriverheadny.viebit.com/player_live.php  
3. Zoom Meeting, log in as follows: 
https://us02web.zoom.us/j/86568814249?pwd=aNYOiuEs6HxbcdsnRxc0tbNHMd8RBj.1 
 
Webinar ID:   865 6881 4249 Passcode:  861009 
Dial by your location: +1 929 205 6099 (New York)  
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE , that the public  electing not to attend in 
person will have an opportunity to  be heard, via Zoom, to make their comments and/or 
raise questions regarding any scheduled  public hearings and resolutions  under 
consideration, as applicable, before the CDA & the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead 
at their respective May 21, 2025 meetings, and further participate in the open comment 
period on any matter at the conclusion of the Agenda.  
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE that the public hearings subject to participation 
via Zoom are as follows:  
 
6:00PM Public Hearing: to consider a special permit application submitted by 
National Grid seeking to upgrade an existing site located at 8 Mill Road, 
Riverhead, NY, SCTM No. 600-120-2-7, with proposed redevelopment includes 
the demolition of two existing buildings, demolition of certain utility structures, 
constructing a new access driveway and apron on Mill Road, creating trailer 
parking spaces for a total of twenty-four (24) CNG trucks, and installing related 
CNG distribution and collection equipment;  
 
6:00 PM Public Hearing: regarding the proposed condemnation of 111 E. Main 
Street, reputed owner, The Place for Learning, Inc., Suffolk County Tax Map 
0600-129-01-11; and 
 
 
2.1
Packet Pg. 11
Communication: 5-21-25 Combined Notice for TB and CDA - 3 Public Hearings  (Notice)
6:05 PM Public Hearing: regarding the proposed condemnation of SNR Bar 25 Corp.’s 
Leasehold Interest to the easterly ground floor rental unit located at 127 East Main 
Street, Riverhead, New York, 11901.  
 
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE , that upon entering the Zoom meeting, you 
will be placed in a virtual audience. From there, you may either passively watch the 
meeting live, or communicate with the moderator/host your request to make a comment 
during the public comment section for PUBLIC HEARINGS, RESOLUTIONS (3 min limit) 
and/or OPEN COMMENTS (3 min limit). To get the attention of the moderator/host, use 
the “CHAT” or “RAISE HAND” feature, then use the “CHAT” feature to inform the 
moderator/host of the following: 
 
1) Name; 2) Hamlet; 3) Public Hearing, Resolution and/or Open Comment topic. 
 
If you are calling in, please dial *9 to “raise your hand”, so we can acknowledge your 
request to speak. 
 
When it is your turn to speak, your status will be temporarily changed so you can be 
unmuted and visible for the comment period. After the comment period, you will be placed 
back in the audience. 
 
All comments/questions offered during the Resolution and Open Comment period will be 
limited to three minutes. Please be patient; your admittance will be based on the volume 
of participants. Any problems or issues getting to the Town Board meeting via telephone 
or computer should be directed to (631) 727-3200 x655.

6.1
Packet Pg. 13
Communication: Letter from Heart of Riverhead Civic - Long Island Science Center  (Correspondence)
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD NOTICE OF PUBLIC HEARING PLEASE TAKE NOTICE that a public hearing will be 
held before the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead at 4 West 2nd Street, Riverhead, New York, on the 
21st day of May, 2025, at or about 6:00 p.m., to consider a special permit application submitted by 
National Grid seeking to upgrade an existing site located at 8 Mill Road, Riverhead, NY, SCTM No. 600-
120-2-7, with proposed redevelopment includes the demolition of two existing buildings, demolition of 
certain utility structures, constructing a new access driveway and apron on Mill Road, creating trailer 
parking spaces for a total of twenty-four (24) CNG trucks, and installing related CNG distribution and 
collection equipment. Dated:  May 8, 2025 Riverhead, New York BY THE ORDER OF THE TOWN BOARD 
OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD JAMES M. WOOTEN, Town Clerk 
 
 
 
 
8.1.a
Packet Pg. 14
Attachment: National Grid Special Permit  (2025-22 : 6:00 PM Public Hearing- National Grid Special Permit)
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
PUBLIC NOTICE 
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board of 
the Town of Riverhead on the 21st day of May, 2025 at 6:00 o'clock in the evening of that day at 
the Town Hall located at 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York pursuant to Article 2 of 
the New York State Eminent Domain Procedure Law with respect to the proposed condemnation 
of 111 E. Main Street, reputed owner, The Place for Learning, Inc., Suffolk County Tax Map 
0600-129-01-11. 
 The proposed acquisition will be for general municipal purposes. 
This acquisition has been determined by the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead, as 
lead agency, to be a Type I action pursuant to 6 NYCRR Part 617.4 (a)(2) and §225-11 B. (10) of 
the Riverhead Town Code as it involves “actions involving commercial or multifamily use 
within a Town of Riverhead Historic District or located within 500 feet of a Town of Riverhead 
Historic District Boundary,” and had undergone mandatory coordinated review among involved 
agencies and the Town Board, as lead agency, has determined that the acquisition is not expected 
to result in any significant adverse environmental impacts and has directed the Planning 
Department on behalf of the Town Board to submit a Negative Declaration to the New York 
State Department of Environmental Conservation Environmental Notice Bulletin. 
Dated:  Riverhead, New York     
 April 17, 2025 
 
 BY THE ORDER OF THE TOWN BOARD 
 OF THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
      JAMES M. WOOTEN, Town Clerk 
 
 
 
 
8.2.a
Packet Pg. 15
Attachment: Reso 317-PUBLIC NOTICE 111 E MAIN CONDEMNATION  (2025-23 : 6:00 PM Public Hearing- Acquisition 111 East Main)
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
NOTICE TO PROPERTY OWNER PURSUANT TO SECTION 202(C)(1) AND (2)  
OF THE NEW YORK EMINENT DOMAIN LAW 
 
BY CERTIFIED MAIL, RETURN RECEIPT REQUESTED 
TO: The Place for Learning, Inc. 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board of 
the Town of Riverhead on the 21st day of May, 2025 at 6:00 o'clock in the evening of that day at 
the Town Hall located at 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York pursuant to Article 2 of 
the New York State Eminent Domain Procedure Law with respect to the proposed  
condemnation of 111 E. Main Street, Riverhead, New York 11901, Suffolk County Tax Map 
0600-129-01-11. 
 The proposed acquisition will be for general municipal purposes. 
This acquisition has been determined by the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead, as 
lead agency, to be a Type I action pursuant to 6 NYCRR Part 617.4 (a)(2) and §225-11 B. (10) of 
the Riverhead Town Code as it involves “actions involving commercial or multifamily use 
within a Town of Riverhead Historic District or located within 500 feet of a Town of Riverhead 
Historic District Boundary,” and had undergone mandatory coordinated review among involved 
agencies and the Town Board, as lead agency, has determined that the acquisition is not expected 
to result in any significant adverse environmental impacts and has directed the Planning 
Department on behalf of the Town Board to submit a Negative Declaration to the New York 
State Department of Environmental Conservation Environmental Notice Bulletin. 
PLEASE TAKE FURTHER NOTICE THAT PROPERTY OWNERS WHO MAY 
SUBSEQUENTLY WISH TO CHALLENGE CONDEMNATION OF THEIR 
PROPERTY VIA JUDICIAL REVIEW MAY DO SO ONLY ON THE BASIS OF 
ISSUES, FACTS, AND OBJECTIONS RAISED AT SUCH HEARING. 
Dated:  Riverhead, New York     
 April 17, 2025

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
PUBLIC NOTICE 
 
 PLEASE TAKE NOTICE, that a public hearing will be held before the Town Board of 
the Town of Riverhead on the 21st day of May, 2025 at 6:05 o'clock in the evening of that day at 
the Town Hall located at 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York pursuant to Article 2 of 
the New York State Eminent Domain Procedure Law with respect to the proposed condemnation 
of SNR Bar 25 Corp.’s Leasehold Interest to the easterly ground floor rental unit located at 127 
East Main Street, Riverhead, New York, 11901.   
 The proposed acquisition will be for general municipal purposes. 
This acquisition has been determined by the Town Board of the Town of Riverhead, as 
lead agency, to be a Type I action pursuant to 6 NYCRR Part 617.4 (a)(2) and §225-11 B. (10) of 
the Riverhead Town Code as it involves “actions involving commercial or multifamily use 
within a Town of Riverhead Historic District or located within 500 feet of a Town of Riverhead 
Historic District Boundary,” and had undergone mandatory coordinated review among involved 
agencies and the Town Board, as lead agency, has determined that the acquisition is not expected 
to result in any significant adverse environmental impacts and has directed the Planning 
Department on behalf of the Town Board to submit a Negative Declaration to the New York 
State Department of Environmental Conservation Environmental Notice Bulletin.

 April 17, 2025

capacity, and 
 
WHEREAS, H2M Architects + Engineers, consulting engineers to the Riverhead 
Water District, has been engaged to perform the required permitting process with the 
New York State Department of Environmental Conservation related to the 
aforementioned project; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Superintended of the Riverhead Water District has requested to 
transfer budgeted expenditures from water improvements to fund the permitting stage of 
this project. Now, therefore be it

following budget adjustment;

TB Resolution 2025-422 
 
AUTHORIZES THE SUPERVISOR TO EXECUTE AGREEMENT WITH TODD 
O’CONNELL ARCHITECT, P.C. FOR  AMBULANCE DISTRICT BUILDING 
RENOVATIONS 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, the Town of Riverhead is desirous of retaining the services of Todd 
O’Connell Architect, P.C. to revise the existing design to meet Axis modular system, new third 
story, full basement and enlarged mezzanine at the Ambulance District building on Osborn 
Avenue, Riverhead, New York (see attached Schedule A) to be used and occupied by RVAC in 
furtherance of it’s services to the Ambulance District and the Town of Riverhead; and  
   WHEREAS, Todd O’Connell Architect, P.C. is ready, willing and able to provide such 
services and has provided a proposal for these in an amount not greater than $11,280.39; and  
WHEREAS, the Town of Riverhead desires to enter into an agreement with Todd 
O’Connell Architect, P.C. to perform these specific services on behalf of the Ambulance 
District.  
 
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board hereby authorizes 
the Supervisor to execute a Professional Services Agreement with Todd O’Connell 
Architect, P.C. in substantially the same form annexed hereto; and be it further,  
 
RESOLVED, that the Town of Riverhead Financial Administrator hereby has the 
authority to establish the appropriate budget for the revenue and expenditure; and be it 
further, 
 
 RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the Office of the Town Attorney and the Accounting Department; and be it 
further,  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a copy of same may be 
obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
SECONDER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

CONSULTANT/PROFESSIONAL SERVICES AGREEMENT 
 
 
This Agreement made the    day of          , 2025, between the TOWN OF RIVERHEAD, 
a municipal corporation organized and existing under the laws of New York, with its 
office located at 4 West Second Street , Riverhead, New York 11901 (hereinafter 
referred to as the “Town”) and Todd O’Connell Architect, P.C. , a company existing 
under the laws of the State of New York  with a principal place of business at 1200 
Veterans Memorial Highway, Suite 120 , Hauppauge, New York 117 88 (hereinafter 
referred to as “Consultant“). 
 
In consideration of the mutual promises herein contained, Town of Riverhead and 
Consultant agree as follows: 
 
1. PROJECT DESCRIPTION 
The Town of Riverhead is proposing a renovation of the  building located at 1111 
Osborn Avenue in Riverhead, New York presently occupied by the Riverhead Volunteer 
Ambulance Corp. in furtherance of services provided for the Ambulance District . The 
Consultant will revise the existing design to meet Axis modular system, new third story, 
full basement and enlarged mezzanine (see attached Schedule A). 
2. SCOPE OF SERVICES 
During the term of this Agreement, Consultant shall furnish services  pursuant to the 
attached Schedule A, including but not limited to the following: 
The Architect will meet with the Client to develop an understanding of the goals of the 
Client with respect to the functional and spatial requirements and overall character of 
the project. 
The Architect will prepare schematic design drawings to illustrate the proposed plan and 
the general character of the exterior of the structure.  
The Architect and Client will meet to discuss the schematic design. Based on these 
discussions, complete schematic design drawings will be prepared to fully illustrate the 
character of the project. 
These services are to be rendered by Consultant as an independent contractor and not 
as an employee of Town.  
3.  TERM OF AGREEMENT 
The Agreement shall be deemed to have commenced on full execution of this 
agreement and terminate on completion of the project. Notwithstanding the above, 
Consultant shall deliver schematic design services and construction documents within 
10.2.a
Packet Pg. 24
Attachment: Todd O’Connell Architect Agreement for RVAC  (2025-422 : Authorizes the Supervisor to Execute Agreement with Todd O’Connell
2 
 
two weeks and four weeks , respectively. The full scope of these deliverables are set 
forth in attached proposal at Schedule A. 
 
4.  PAYMENT 
For these services, Town will pay Consultant a  flat fee of ELEVEN THOUSAND TWO 
HUNDRED EIGHTY DOLLARS AND THIRTY NINE CENTS ($11,280.39) regarding 
scope of services as set forth in the attached Schedule A, which shall be paid as 
follows: Retainer with authorized signature ($7,030.39) and Completion of Design 
Drawings ($4,250.00). 
 
The Town shall not have any liability for any other expenses or costs incurred by 
Consultant except for expenses expressly provided for in the attached schedule  A. 
Consultant shall not incur any expenses in Town’s behalf except for those items 
expressly provided for and limited to the amount set forth in the attached schedule  A.  
Invoices for services and reimbursable expenses shall contain the following statement 
signed by Consultant, or if this Agreement is with a firm, an officer or authorized 
representative of the firm:  “I hereby certify, to the best of my knowledge and belief, that 
this invoice is correct, and that all items invoiced are based upon actual costs incurred 
or services rendered consistent with the terms of the professional services agreement.”  
Each invoice for reimbursable expenses shall be supported by:  (a) an itemized 
description of expenses claimed; (b) pertinent information relative to the expenses; and 
(c) attached receipts.  Invoices shall reference this Agreement or otherwise be identified 
in such a manner as Town may reasonably require.  Consultant shall produce an 
invoice after each completed service visit, and such invoice(s) shall be due net thirty 
(30) days from the invoicing date. 
 
5.  RIGHTS TO DOCUMENTS OR DATA 
All information and data, regardless of form, generated in the performance of, or 
delivered under this Agreement, as well as any information provided to Consultant by 
Town, shall be and remain the sole property of Town.  Consultant shall keep all such 
information and data in confidence and not disclose or use it for any purpose other than 
in performing this Agreement, except with Town’s prior written approval.  In the event 
that the legal right in any data and information generated in the performance of this 
Agreement does not vest in Town by law, Consultant hereby agrees and assigns to 
Town such legal rights in all such data and information.  Final payment shall not be due 
hereunder until after receipt by Town of such complete document and data file, or a 
certification that there is no such information created by the services performed under 
this Agreement, and receipt of all information and data which is the property of Town.  
These obligations shall survive the termination of this Agreement. 
 
6.  PUBLICITY 
Consultant shall not, without the prior written consent of Town, in any manner advertise 
or publish the fact that Town has entered into this Agreement with Consultant.  
Consultant shall not, without the prior written consent of the Town, provide, release or 
make available for inspection any documents, data, written material of any kind without 
10.2.a
Packet Pg. 25
Attachment: Todd O’Connell Architect Agreement for RVAC  (2025-422 : Authorizes the Supervisor to Execute Agreement with Todd O’Connell
3 
 
the prior written consent of at least three members of the Town board or by resolution of 
the Town Board.   
            
7.  ASSIGNMENT AND SUBCONTRACTING 
Performance of any part of this Agreement may not be subcontracted nor assigned 
without, in each case, the prior written consent of at least three members of the Town 
Board or by resolution of the Town Board. 
 
8.  TERMINATION 
This Agreement may be terminated at any time and for any reason by either party upon 
30 days written notice to the other party.  In the event of such termination, Town shall 
have no further obligation to Consultant except to make any payments which may have 
become due for services rendered under this Agreement.  
 
9.  RECORDS 
Consultant shall keep accurate records of the time spent in the performance of services 
hereunder.  The Town shall, until the expiration of three years after final payment under 
this Agreement, have access to and the right to examine any directly pertinent books, 
documents, papers and records of Consultant involving transactions related to this 
Agreement. 
 
10.  CHANGES 
The Town, by resolution of the Town Board or written request by at least three members 
of the Town Board, may, at any time by written notice to Consultant, issue additional 
instructions, require additional services or direct the omission of services covered by 
this Agreement.  It is understood and agreed that major revisions to drawings when 
such revisions are inconsistent with prior instructions and approvals, changes in project 
scope, value engineering revisions resulting in changes in project scope and budget 
that are inconsistent with prior instructions and approvals, local laws & regulations or 
other services requested beyond those described above shall constitute additional 
services and such compensation for additional services could be separately negotiated 
lump sum amounts for specific tasks or billed hourly per the attached Schedule A. In 
such event, there will be made an equitable adjustment in price and time of 
performance, but any claim for such an adjustment must be made within 15 days of the 
receipt of such written notice.  In the event that the Consultant determines that a change 
order is required, Consultant shall obtain written approval of the Town, by resolution or 
written consent of at least three members of the Town Board, and if the change shall 
require the payment of additional compensation, Consultant must obtain the written 
approval of three members of the Town Board or resolution of the Town Board for the 
additional compensation prior to commencement of work regarding the change order.  It 
is agreed and understood that no oral agreement, conversation, or understanding 
between the Consultant and the Town, its departments, officers, agents and employees 
shall affect or modify any of the terms or obligations of this Agreement or schedules 
annexed hereto and made a part hereof.

11.  NOTICES 
Any notice shall be considered as having been given:  (i) to Town of Riverhead if mailed 
by certified mail, postage prepaid to Town of Riverhead, Attention:  Office of the Town 
Attorney, 4 West Second Street, Riverhead, New York 11901; or (ii) to Consultant if 
mailed by certified mail, postage prepaid to Todd O’Connell Architect, P.C., at 1200 
Veterans Memorial Highway, Suite 120, Hauppauge, New York 11788.  
 
12.  COMPLIANCE WITH LAWS 
Consultant shall comply with all applicable federal, state and local laws and ordinances 
and regulations in the performance of its services under this Agreement.  Consultant will 
notify Town immediately if Consultant’s work for Town becomes the subject of a 
government audit or investigation.  Consultant will promptly notify Town if Consultant is 
indicted, suspended or debarred.  Consultant represents that Consultant has not been 
convicted of fraud or any other felony arising out of a contract with any local, state or 
federal agency.  In carrying out the work required hereunder, Consultant agrees not to 
make any communication to or appearance before any person in the executive or 
legislative branches of the local, state or federal government for the purpose of 
influencing or attempting to influence any such persons in connection with the award, 
extension, continuation, renewal, amendment or modification of any contract or 
agreement.  Consultant may perform professional or technical services that are 
rendered directly in the preparation, submission or negotiation activities preceding 
award of a Town agreement/contract or to meet requirements imposed by law as a 
condition for receiving the award but only to the extent specifically detailed in the 
statement of work.  Professional and technical services are limited to advice and 
analysis directly applying Consultant’s professional and technical discipline. 
 
13. INSURANCE, INDEMNITY AND LIABILITY        
Consultant shall maintain Comprehensive General Liability Insurance and, if applicable, 
worker’s compensation insurance, as follows: 
 
Worker’s Compensation Insurance.  Consultant shall maintain during the term of 
this Agreement worker’s compensation insurance for all of Consultant’s 
employees providing scope of services pursuant to this Agreement, which shall 
name the Town of Riverhead and Riverhead Volunteer Ambulance Corp. as 
additional insureds. In addition, in the event Consultant  utilizes sub-contractor(s) 
regarding scope of services, sub-contractor(s) shall also be required to maintain 
worker’s compensation insurance for each employees providing scope of 
services pursuant to this Agreement which shall also name the Town of 
Riverhead and Riverhead Volunteer Ambulance Corp.  as additional insured, 
unless such sub -contractors are insured pursuant to Consultant’s worker’s 
compensation insurance policy. 
 
Commercial General Liability Insurance and Umbrella Liability Insurance:  
Consultant shall maintain during the term of this Agreement commercial general 
liability insurance and umbrella liability insurance  regarding scope of services as

Except for the indemnification obligations herein, Consultant’s liability with respect to the 
services performed hereunder shall be limited to the written warranty remedies

15.  CONFLICT OF INTEREST 
Consultant hereby represents and covenants that neither it nor any of its employees or 
representatives has or shall have, directly or indirectly, any agreement or arrangement 
with any official, employee or representative of the Town of Riverhead which any such 
official, employee, representative shall receive either directly or indirectly anything of 
value whether monetary or otherwise as the result of or in connection with any actual or 
contemplated application before any department of the Town, contract with the Town for 
sale of any product or service.  Consultant further represents and covenants that neither 
it nor any of its employees or representatives has offered or shall offer any gratuity to 
the Town, its officers, employees, agents or representatives with a view toward 
obtaining this Agreement or securing favorable treatment with respect thereto.  
Consultant further represents that it will not engage in any activity which presents a 
conflict of interest in light of its relationship with Town. 
 
16.  DISCLOSURE 
The Town shall have the right, in its discretion, to disclose the terms and conditions of 
this Agreement (as it may be amended from time to time), including but not limited to 
amounts paid pursuant hereto, to agencies of the local, state and federal government. 
 
17.  DISPUTES 
If Consultant fails to perform any of its obligations hereunder in accordance with the 
terms hereof, then after reasonable notice to Consultant not to exceed thirty (30) days, 
and an opportunity for Consultant to cure such failure (except in case of emergency), 
the Town may (but shall not be obligated to) cure such failure at the expense of the 
Consultant, and the amount incurred by the Town on demand.  Notwithstanding the 
above, any dispute arising under this Agreement which is not settled by Agreement of 
the parties may be settled by appropriate legal proceedings. The Town and Consultant 
agree that prior to resorting to litigation, the matter be submitted to mediation upon the 
written request of either  party and the results of such mediation shall only be binding 
upon agreement of each party to be bound thereby. The costs of mediation proceedings 
shall be shared equally by both parties. Pending any decision, appeal or judgment in 
such proceedings or the settlement of any dispute arising under this Agreement, 
Consultant shall proceed diligently with the performance of this Agreement in 
accordance with the decision of Town.

The Architect is to be retained to provide the following services as they relate to the above-referenced 
project. 
ARTICLE I: BASIC SERVICES 
1.1 Programming Phase 
1.1.1 The Architect will meet with the Client to develop an understanding of the goals of the Client with 
respect to the functional and spatial requirements and overall character of the project. 
1.2 Design Phase 
1.2.1 The Architect will prepare schematic design drawings to illustrate the proposed plan and the 
general character of the exterior of the structure. 
1.2.2 The Architect and Client will meet to discuss the schematic design. Based on these discussions, 
complete schematic design drawings will be prepared to fully illustrate the character of the 
project. 
ARTICLE II: CLIENT RESPONSIBILITIES 
2.1 The Client shall provide full and accurate information regarding requirements for the project. 
2.2 The Client shall furnish a certified land survey of the site as well as any other available 
documentation for the property. The Client may be required to provide additional documentation for 
filing with the appropriate agencies including but not limited to a copy of the deed and tax bills for the 
property. 
2.3 If the Client becomes aware of any development that affects the scope or timing of the services or 
becomes aware of any faults or defects in the project. or noncompliance with the Construction 
Documents, the Client shall give the Architect prompt notice thereof. 
ARTICLE Ill: COMPENSATION 
3.1 Todd O'Connell Architect, PC will require a flat fee of$ 11,280.39 for the above services to be paid as 
follows: 
Retainer with authorized signature 
Completion of Design Drawings 
$7,030.39 
$4,250.00 
3.2 Payments to the Architect shall be due upon receipt of invoice. After thirty (30) days, unpaid invoices 
shall accrue interest at the rate of 1.5% monthly (18% per annum).

ARTICLE V: GENERAL CONDITIONS 
5.1. The standard of care for all professional services performed or furnished by the Architect under this 
agreement will be the skill and care used by members of architect's profession practicing under 
similar circumstances at the same time and in the same locality based on the standard of care 
provided by others in the industry. The Architect makes no warranties, express or implied, under this 
agreement or otherwise, in connection with architectural services. 
5.2. The Client and Architect each agree to indemnify and hold the other harmless, and their respective 
officers, employees, agents and representatives, from and against liability for all claims, losses, 
damages, or expenses, including reasonable attorneys' fees, to the extent such claims, losses, 
damages, or expenses are caused by the indemnifying party's negligent acts, errors or omissions. In 
the event claims, losses, damages or expenses are caused by the joint or concurrent negligence of 
The Client and Architect, they shall be borne by each party in proportion to its negligence. 
5.3. Neither party shall be deemed in default of this agreement to the extent that any delay or failure in the 
performance of its obligations results from any cause beyond its reasonable control and without 
negligence. 
5.4. The Client and Architect agree that they shall first submit any and all unsettled claims, counterclaims, 
disputes, and other matters in question between them arising out of or relating to this agreement to 
mediation in accordance with the Construction Industry Mediation Rules of the American Arbitration 
Association, effective as of the date of this agreement.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-424 
 
AUTHORIZES HIGHWAY SUPERINTENDENT EXPENDITURES 2025-2026 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, New York State Highway Law §142(1)(a) provides that the Town 
Highway Superintendent may, with approval of the Town Board, purchase equipment, 
tools and other implements to be used for highway maintenance, construction, 
reconstruction and/or snow removal; and  
 
WHEREAS, New York State Highway Law §142(1)(a) also provides that the 
Town Board may authorize the Highway Superintendent to purchase equipment, tools 
and other implements to be used for highway maintenance, construction or 
reconstruction, snow ploughs or other devices for the removal of snow from the 
highways from moneys appropriated for that purpose without prior approval  in an 
amount or amounts to be fixed, from time to time, by the board; and  
 
WHEREAS, the Superintendent of Highways has requested Town Board 
authorization to spend up to $75,000.00 annually for equipment, tools and implements 
without prior Town Board approval in order to provide an opportunity to purchase used 
equipment at state, county and municipal auctions and other such equipment, tools and 
implements to be used for highway maintenance, construction, reconstruction and/or 
snow removal, with the condition that all such purchases comply with New York State 
General Municipal Law §103.  
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED that the Superintendent of Highways be 
and is hereby authorized to spend up to $75,000.00 annually for equipment, tools and 
other implements  without prior approval of the Town Board for 2025 and 2026; and be 
it further,  
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
Resolution to the Highway Department, Purchasing Department, Accounting 
Department and Office of the Town Attorney; and be it further  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Joann Waski, Councilwoman

AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-425 
 
SETS HOURS FOR TOWN BEACHES 
 
Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Kern 
 
WHEREAS, Section 211-21 of the Riverhead Town Code directs the Town Board 
to establish the hours and period of time a public bathing beach shall be open 
WHEREAS, public bathing beaches are defined as shoreline areas owned, 
maintained, or operated by the Town of Riverhead for the use and enjoyment of 
residents and visitors, which typically include designated swimming areas with 
appropriate safety measures, lifeguards on duty during operating hours, and may offer 
amenities such as restrooms and changing facilities 
RESOLVED, This Town Board sets the hours for all public bathing beaches to be 
open weekends from May 24 to June 29 and open seven days a week from June 30 
until, and including, Labor Day during the hours 11am until 6pm 
RESOLVED, all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Kenneth Rothwell, Councilman 
SECONDER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-426 
 
SETS HOURS FOR TOWN BEACH PARKING LOTS 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, Section 211-21 of the Riverhead Town Code directs the Town Board 
to establish the hours the town beach parking lots shall be open. 
  
WHEREAS, public bathing beaches are defined as shoreline areas owned, 
maintained, or operated by the Town of Riverhead for the use and enjoyment of 
residents and visitors, and which typically include adjacent areas for the parking of 
vehicles. 
  
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, This Town Board hereby sets and 
establishes that the hours for parking of vehicles at Town Beach parking lots with a valid 
Riverhead Town beach permit and/ or fishing license properly displayed shall be 
between the hours of 6am until 10pm daily and that overnight parking of vehicles shall 
be prohibited; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the Office of the Town Attorney, the Recreation Department, the 
Engineering Department and the Riverhead Town Police Department; and be it further, 
  
RESOLVED, all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
SECONDER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

successfully licensed by the New York State Department of Health as a Water 
Treatment Plant Operator IIB and have completed the required traineeship as per the 
Suffolk County Department of Civil Service; and 
 
WHEREAS, Civil Service regulations require that a Water Treatment Plant

license may be appointed to the position of Water Treatment Plant Operator IIB without 
further examination.

appointment of Paul Caparros to the position of Water Treatment Plant Operator IIB and 
changes his salary from Group 9, Step 3A of the Operational and Technical Salary 
Schedule which is $56,853.28 per annum to Group 15, Step 5 of the same schedule 
which is $65,220.27 per annum. 
 
RESOLVED, that a copy of this resolution be forwarded to payroll and Town Hall 
Departments may review and obtain a copy of this resolution from the electronic storage 
device, and if needed, a certified copy of same can be obtained from the office of the

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-429 
 
RATIFIES THE PROVISIONAL APPOINTMENT OF AN EMPLOYEE TO 
WASTEWATER TREATMENT PLANT OPERATOR 4A 
 
Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Kern 
 
WHEREAS, Tim Allen previously served as Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant 
Operator IIIA, and was individually and internally designated as the Wastewater District 
Deputy Superintendent up until his appointment as Sewer District Superintendent 
effective March 22, 2025, therefore creating a vacancy in the Wastewater District 
Deputy Superintendent position; and 
 
WHEREAS, due to the title restructure  and reclassification  of the Wastewater 
District Superintendent position, the Town also requested a reclassification of the title 
that will be internally designated as the Deputy Sewer Superintendent  and the Suffolk 
County Department of Civil Service reviewed and approved such request and changed 
the title from Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator IIIA to Wastewater 
Treatment Plant Operator 4A; and 
 
WHEREAS, on May 12, 2025 the Suffolk County Department of Civil Service 
confirmed that there was no existing list for the title of Wastewater Treatment Plant 
Operator 4A; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town desires to promote and appoint Brian Cybulski, current 
Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator IIIA  to the provisional title of Wastewater 
Treatment Plant Operator 4A, which will be internally designated as Wastewater District 
Deputy Superintendent effective May 22, 2025  based upon his lengthy service and 
commitment to the Town of Riverhead, experience , and qualifying license from the 
State of New York Department of Environmental Conservation.  
 
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED , that the Town Board of the Town of 
Riverhead does hereby ratify the provisional appointment of Brian Cybulski from Senior 
Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator IIIA to the title of Wastewater Treatment Plant 
Operator 4A of the Riverhead Sewer District, which shall be internally designated as the 
Wastewater District Deputy Superintendent effective May 22, 2025; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk be and is hereby authorized to forward a copy 
of this resolution to the Riverhead Sewer District Superintendent, Timothy Allen, Sewer 
District Deputy Superintendent Brian Cybulski, the Accounting Department  and payroll; 
and be it further,  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of 
same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.

TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-430 
 
SETTING TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF EMPLOYMENT FOR DEPUTY SEWER 
DISTRICT SUPERINTENDENT 
 
Councilman Kern offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Merrifield 
 
WHEREAS, the Town of Riverhead desires to provide the Deputy Wastewater 
District Superintendent, Brian Cybulski, with written terms and conditions of 
employment in order to enhance 
the administrative stability and continuity within the 
Town, which the Town believes generally improves the quality of its overall mission; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town believes that written terms and conditions of employment 
are necessary to specifically describe their relationship and to serve as the basis of 
effective communication between them as they fulfill their governance and 
administrative functions in the operation of the Town.  
 
 NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town of Riverhead wishes to 
set the terms and conditions for the employment of Brian Cybulski as Deputy 
Wastewater District Superintendent  and authorizes the Town Supervisor to enter into 
an agreement setting forth terms and conditions of employment with Cybulski in a form 
substantially similar to the agreement attached hereto; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby directed to forward a copy of this 
resolution to the Accounting Department, Payroll, Sewer District, Personnel Director and 
the Office of the Town Attorney; and be it further,  
 
 RESOLVED, all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
SECONDER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

Agreement made and entered into this day of May ____ 2025, between THE 
TOWN OF 
RIVERHEAD, County of Suffolk, State of New York, (hereinafter referred to as the 
"Town ") 
and Brian Cybulski (hereinafter “Cybulski.”) 
WITNESSETH: 
WHEREAS, the Town desires to provide Cybulski in his capacity as Deputy Wastewater 
District Superintendent with written terms and conditions of employment in order to enhance 
administrative stability and continuity within the Town, which the Town believes generally 
improves the quality of its overall mission; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town and Cybulski believe that written terms and conditions of 
employment are necessary to describe specifically their relationship and to serve as the basis of 
effective communication between them as they fulfill their governance and administrative functions 
in the operation of the Town; and 
 
WHEREAS, this Agreement supersedes all prior agreements between the parties; and 
 
WHEREAS, this Agreement cannot be, in whole or in part, amended orally by the parties. 
 
NOW THEREFORE, in exchange of the mutual covenants and considerations, it is agreed 
that the terms and conditions of employment of Cybulski while employed in his position as Deputy 
Wastewater District Superintendent shall be as follows:  
 
ARTICLE I 
DURATION 
This Agreement shall be effective as of  May _____ , 2025 and shall continue in full force 
and effect during the period of time Cybulski serves as the Deputy Wastewater District 
Superintendent or until subsequently altered by Town Board Resolution. The terms and conditions 
set forth in Articles Il, Ill and IV with respect to personal time, vacation, sick time and longevity 
shall be prorated for the 2025 calendar year. 
 
 ARTICLE II 
 
 RECOGNITION 
 
1.  The Town recognizes Cybulski’s right to bargain for the terms and conditions of his 
employment with the Town.  Both parties acknowledge that this Agreement is personal to Cybulski 
and shall not inure to his successor.  Such recognition is for the period of t his Agreement or 
extensions hereof.  
 
10.10.a
Packet Pg. 54
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 2 of 9 
 
2. Cybulski affirms that he does not assert the right to strike against the Town, or to assist or 
participate in any such strike, picket, job action or any work slowdown. 
 
3.  The Town recognizes  Cybulski’s right to designate a representative to appear on his 
behalf to discuss salaries, working conditions, grievances and disputes relative to the terms and 
conditions of t his Agreement and to confer with Cybulski during working hours.  The 
representative's activities shall not disrupt the orderly and smooth operation of Town government. 
 
 ARTICLE III 
 
 HOURS OF WORK 
 
1.  Cybulski’s minimum basic work week shall be  40 hours per week.  There shall be no 
maximum number of hours of work per week. Cybulski shall not receive additional compensation 
for holiday pay.  Cybulski is not entitled to earn, accrue, or be paid for overtime or compensatory 
time.  
 
2.  Cybulski shall be en titled to the same paid holidays as the Employees under his 
supervision. 
 
3. (a) Five (5) days personal leave will be granted.  
 
    (b)  Personal leave may not be accumulated and must be used within the calendar year 
earned, except that unused personal days at the end of each year shall be converted to sick time 
and may be used as sick time, subject to all the rules and pertaining to sick time. 
 
    (c)  Personal leave must be approved by his Department Head or Town S upervisor. 
Cybulski must request such leave at least forty eight (48) hours in advance unless the personal leave 
is deemed to be an emergency of which he had no prior knowledge, in which case  Cybulski must 
notify his Department Head of such absence. Failure to notify h is supervisor of his absence will 
result in loss of pay for the day's absence. 
 
4.  Funeral Leave.  Cybulski shall be entitled to four (4) consecutive working days leave of 
absence computed either from the day of death or the day following death, at Cybulski’s option, for 
the death of Cybulski’s spouse, child (including adopted children), father, mother, brother, sister, 
parents, parents-in-law, grandparents, grandparents-in-law, grandchildren, daughter-in-law, brother-
in-law, sister-in-law, son-in-law, or stepchild. 
 
5.  Jury Service. Cybulski will be paid his regular salary while performing jury service upon 
documentary proof being filed with the Supervisor. Cybulski shall endorse the jury salary checks to 
the Town.  Travel allowance or mileage compensation checks for jury service are to be retained by    
Cybulski. 
 
10.10.a
Packet Pg. 55
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 3 of 9 
 
6.  Court Appearance. Cybulski absence by reason of appearance as a defendant or witness 
on behalf of the Town in any court action involving the Town will be approved by the Town 
Supervisor for the number of days necessary. Cybulski shall not lose any salary there from. 
 
7.  Parentage Leave.  Cybulski shall receive a parentage leave as defined in the 2022-2025 
CSEA contract, Article III, Section 5. 
 
 ARTICLE IV 
 
 VACATIONS 
 
1.  Cybulski shall be entitled to 20 working days' vacation (January 1 to December 31).  This 
shall be prorated in 2025.   
 
2.  Cybulski, upon request, shall be paid his vacation pay prior to the vacation, providing he 
shall have given three (3) weeks' written notice to the Supervisor. 
 
3.  Upon retirement or termination of service, except for cause,  Cybulski shall be 
compensated, in cash, for any accumulated vacation not to exceed 60 days. 
 
4.  Cybulski may carry over any unused vacation days from one (1) year into the following 
year, but in no event shall Cybulski carry over more than sixty (60) vacation days from one year to 
the next. 
 
            5 Cybulski, at his option, shall be entitled to make an election to work the current year's 
allotted vacation time. Cybulski must provide written notification to the Supervisor of the 
exercising of this option not fewer than thirty (30) days prior to the date of which payment is 
requested. The Supervisor is to acknowledge receipt of this notification to the payroll personnel 
prior to payment. Payment is to be processed during the next overtime run. Payment will be the 
same method as outlined in the 2012-2015 Superior Officers' Contract, Article IX, Section B, 
except that the buyback shall be in blocks of three days per month. “In addition, Cybulski must 
advise the Town in writing, by no later than September 1 prior to the year in which the election is 
being made, on a form to be prepared by the Town, of the total minimum and the maximum dollar 
amounts of eligible vacation time and/or sick leave, as appropriate, that the employee will buyout 
and for which he will be paid in the next fiscal year. If the employee does not comply with t his 
requirement, then the employee will not be eligible for any accrued time buyout in the next fiscal 
year.”  
 
ARTICLE V 
 
SICK LEAVE 
 
1.  Sick leave is absence necessitated by Cybulski’s illness or other physical disability.  Sick 
10.10.a
Packet Pg. 56
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 4 of 9 
 
leave will be accumulated at the rate of one and one-half (1 1/2) days per month or (eighteen  [18] 
days per year), total accumulated sick leave of three hundred (300) days.  After three hundred (300) 
days, additional paid sick leave may be granted in the sole discretion of the Town Board.  In order to 
receive sick leave, Cybulski shall, when absent because of sickness for more than three (3) days, 
furnish the Supervisor, when requested by him/her, with a medical certificate.  Failure to furnish a 
medical certificate will result in loss of pay for absent days.  The Town Board, in its discretion, may 
request a physical examination of Cybulski before his return to work. 
 
2.  Cybulski, or his legal representative, upon retirement or severance, is en titled to cash 
payment for accumulated sick leave.  Said payment shall be paid in a lump sum the value of his 
accumulated and unused sick leave to the extent of one hundred (100%) percent of the first two 
hundred and eighty (280) days thereof. 
 
3. The parties mutually agree that excessive absenteeism due to abuse of sick leave should 
be discouraged. Therefore, the Town may request a doctor's certificate from chronic abusers of 
sick leave (e.g., numerous illness absences even though the Cybulski has accumulated sick leave), 
regardless of the length of the illness.  Cybulski submitting a claim based on a false statement, or 
covering a period during which the employee was not actually disabled, will be considered as 
abusing the sick leave provision. E m p l o y e es  who abuse the sick leave provision shall be 
subject to disciplinary action. 
 
4. Cybulski may elect to reduce the sick time accrued under paragraph "1" one by filing a 
written election with the Supervisor one (1) month prior to payment.  Buy-out shall be in lots of 
ten (10) sick days. No buy-out shall be permitted unless at the time of election Cybulski has 
accumulated at least fifty (50) sick days. The rate of pay shall be calculated at the time of payment 
based on a two hundred sixty (260) day work year. If Cybulski "buys-out" sick leave, he shall be 
permitted to re-accumulate sick days to a maximum of three hundred (300) days for use in the event 
of illness, but those days may not be re-accumulated for payment purposes. In addition, Cybulski    
 must advise the Town in writing, by no later than September 1 prior to the year in which the election 
is being made, on a form to be prepared by the Town, of the total minimum and the maximum dollar 
amounts of eligible vacation time and/or sick leave, as appropriate, that the Cybulski will buyout and 
for which he will be paid in the next fiscal year. If the Cybulski does not comply with t his 
requirement, then the Cybulski will not be eligible for any accrued time buyout in the next fiscal 
year. 
ARTICLE VI 
 
GRIEVANCE PROCEDURE 
 
1.  Consideration of Grievance. 
 
A grievance by Cybulski shall be made, in writing, to the Town Board.  Upon receipt of the 
grievance, the Town Board may request Cybulski to submit any agreed statement of facts or his 
version of the facts, or any other documents that the Town Board may deem pertinent to the 
10.10.a
Packet Pg. 57
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 5 of 9 
 
determination of the appeal. 
 
The Town Board shall conduct a hearing within twenty (20) business days of receipt of an 
appeal.  Within twenty (20) business days after the hearing, the Town Board shall make a decision 
based on its findings and advise Cybulski.  The decision of the Town Board shall be final and all 
parties bound thereby. 
 
2.  Time of Hearings. 
 
All discussions and hearings shall, so far as practicable, be conducted during working hours. 
 
3.  Representation. 
 
Cybulski shall have the right at all times to representation of his choosing. 
 
4.  Limitations. 
 
If a grievance occurs and cannot be resolved immediately, Cybulski shall obey all directives 
and shall present the grievance as soon thereafter as practicable.  Grievances which are not presented 
within ten (10) days of the occurrence shall be deemed to have been abandoned. 
 
5.  Withdrawn Grievances. 
 
Cybulski may withdraw a grievance at any point in the grievance procedure. 
 
ARTICLE VII 
 
PENSION AND LONGEVITY 
 
Cybulski represents that he is a member of the New York State Employees Retirement 
System.  As a Tier VI Cybulski, he is a participant in the Article 1 4 or Article 15 Coordinated 
Retirement Plan. 
 
Longevity payments shall be based on the present year’s salary and the percentages 
shall be taken there from.  Cybulski shall be paid longevity based on the following schedule: 
 
Four percent (4%) of base pay after ten (10) years of continuous service with 
the Town.  
Six percent (6%) of base pay after fifteen (15) years of continuous service 
with the Town.  
. 
Seven percent (7%) of base pay after eighteen (18) years of continuous 
service with the Town.

Packet Pg. 58
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 6 of 9 
 
 
ARTICLE VIII 
 
HEALTH INSURANCE 
 
1.  The Town shall pay, on  Cybulski’s behalf, one hundred (100%) percent of the cost of 
either the individual or family coverage for hospitalization under the Town Health Insurance 
Program.  The Town shall pay for one hundred (100%) percent coverage for Cybulski if he retires 
from the Town and the Town shall also pay to the extent of fifty (50%) percent coverage on the 
premiums for his family. 
 
If Cybulski and his spouse, if employed through the Town, are currently receiving (or are 
eligible to receive) family health benefits through the Town, only one will be permitted to continue 
to receive family level coverage.  In this event, the person whose coverage changes from family to 
individual or no coverage will be entitled to the health insurance buy-out, provided that he/he:  (1) 
has submitted to the Town documentation showing that he/he has health insurance coverage other 
than through the New York State Health Insurance Plan (NYSHIP); and (b) remains in changed 
status for a period of 12 consecutive months.  The 12-month period will coincide with the annual 
option transfer period.   Payment will be made annually during the June or December first following 
the end of the 12-month period, provided that Cybulski or his spouse remains in the changed status. 
Cybulski may reinstate coverage within the 12-month period if he/he experiences a qualifying event 
and has submitted to the Town adequate documentation of that event, consistent with the rules and 
regulations of the Town’s health insurance plan and applicable laws and regulations.   
 
At retirement, the former employee who is otherwise eligible for family retiree health 
insurance coverage through the Town but for the operation of t his provision shall continue to be 
ineligible for family retiree health insurance coverage through the Town.  However, during 
retirement, the former employee may reinstate his/her own family health insurance coverage, if the 
former employee has dependents as defined in the Plan, in the event of an emergency causing the 
loss of the other person’s Town health insurance, consistent with the rules and regulations of the 
Town’s health insurance plan and applicable laws and regulations. 
 
In the event that Cybulski’s employment with the Town should terminate, he shall have the 
option, at his own expense, to participate in the Town Health Insurance Program , consistent with 
applicable laws, rules and regulations.   
 
The service requirement for receipt of health insurance in retirement shall be ten  
consecutive years of service with the Town. However, if Cybulski leaves Town service he 
must continue with NYSHIP in vested status by paying the entire cost of coverage, or by being 
enrolled as an e m p l o y e e at a subsequent participating agency or by being enrolled as a 
dependent on a NYSHIP policy in order to retain eligibility for retiree health benefits through 
the Town. If Cybulski leaves to work for another NYSHIP employer, he is not eligible for 
retiree health insurance if he vests with the second employer 
10.10.a
Packet Pg. 59
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 7 of 9 
 
2.  The Town shall pay, on  Cybulski’s behalf, one hundred (100%) percent of the cost of 
either the individual or family plan for dental coverage under the Riverhead Town Dental Plan.  If 
Cybulski and his spouse, if employed through the Town, are currently receiving (or are eligible to 
receive) family dental insurance benefits through the Town, only one will be permitted to continue to 
receive family level coverage.  In t his event, the person whose coverage changes from family to 
individual coverage or no coverage  will be entitled to the dental insurance buy -out.  Should that 
person choose to decline to receive individual coverage, then that person will be eligible for the buy-
out of the individual coverage. 
 
3.  The Town shall pay, on  Cybulski’s behalf, one hundred (100%) percent of the cost of 
either the individual or family plan for optical coverage under the Riverhead Town Optical Plan.  If 
Cybulski and his spouse, if employed through the Town, are currently receiving (or are eligible to 
receive) family optical insurance benefits through the Town, only one will be permitted to continue 
to receive family level coverage.  In this event, the person whose coverage changes from family to 
individual coverage or no coverage will be entitled to the optical insurance buy -out.  Should that 
person choose to decline to receive individual coverage, then that person will be eligible for the buy-
out of the individual coverage. 
 
4.  The Town will insure Cybulski life in accordance with the maximum death benefit 
provided by the Employees Retirement System for Tier VI members.   
 
5. Cybulski, at his option, may elect not to accept the Town's hospitalization coverage for 
a period of not less than one calendar year and receive the following payment during the first full 
pay period of each year the election is made: $1,650 if Cybulski changes from family to no 
coverage; $900 if Cybulski changes from family to individual coverage; $750 if Cybulski 
changes from individual to no coverage. Also, at his option, Cybulski may elect not to accept the 
dental coverage for a period of not less than one calendar year and receive the following payment 
during the first full pay period of each year the election is made:  $230 if Cybulski changes from 
family to no coverage; $150 if Cybulski changes from family to individual coverage; $80 if 
Cybulski changes from individual to no coverage. Also, at his option, Cybulski may elect not to 
accept the optical coverage for a period of not less than one calendar year and receive a payment 
of twenty five dollars ($25.00) during the first full pay period of each year the election is made.  
Cybulski must sign an application form each year and said application shall include an 
acknowledgment that he is covered under another plan. 
 
  
 ARTICLE IX 
 
 GENERAL PROVISIONS 
 
1.  The Town agrees to provide legal counsel to defend Cybulski in any action arising out of 
an assault on Cybulski on Town business, and the Town hereby agrees to defend, indemnify, and 
hold Cybulski harmless for any and all acts performed for the Town, its agents and employees, 
10.10.a
Packet Pg. 60
Attachment: Cybulski Agreement Deputy Wastewater Superintendent Terms and Conditions  (2025-430 : Setting Terms and Conditions of
 
 
Page 8 of 9 
 
including but not limited to preparation, certification and sealing of plans prepared exclusively for 
the Town, its agents and employees, provided  Cybulski was acting within the scope of his 
employment.  In the event that Cybulski is appointed, authorized or directed by the Town or one of 
its agencies to represent it as a member of the board of directors of an organization or agency, then 
he shall be covered by the provisions of Public Officers Law Section 18 and Town Code Sections 
15-1 and 15-2 pertaining to the defense and indemnification of officers and employees of public 
entities, provided  Cybulski is otherwise eligible for coverage pursuant to the terms of those 
provisions. 
 
2.  If Cybulski is injured or assaulted in the course of employment, he shall receive 100% of 
his salary for the first six months during which he is absent from work, and 85% of his salary for any 
time beyond that period, until such time as his application for reinstatement to full duty status, or, in 
the event of permanent disability, his application for a disability pension be finally determined or by 
a physician's examination determining no further disability, whichever comes first.  If Cybulski is 
injured on the job and reports the same to the Supervisor, and has to be absent from work, no days 
shall be deducted from his sick leave for such injury.  If Cybulski receives a compensation check for 
lost time due to a compensable injury, he shall endorse his check over to the Town.  The above shall 
apply if Cybulski was acting within the scope of his employment.  Nothing contained herein shall in 
any way be deemed to restrict the Town’s right to separate Cybulski pursuant to the provisions of 
Civil Service Law Sections 71-73. 
 
3.  A leave of absence, without pay, may be granted to Cybulski in the discretion of the Town 
Board for a maximum of six (6) months, upon written application therefore and good cause shown. 
 
4.  If Cybulski is absent without leave or without due notification to the Supervisor, he shall 
suffer loss of pay for the days of such absence.  
 
5.  Cybulski will be paid every two (2) weeks on second Thursday after the pay-period ends.   
 
6.  Upon Cybulski request to examine his official employment personnel file, he may be 
permitted to do so at the discretion of the Town Board.  Any material classified as confidential shall 
not be subject to duplication by Cybulski, but he shall have an opportunity to read said material and 
make a written reply, which shall be inserted in his personnel folder. 
 
7.  To the extent permitted by the U.S. Internal Revenue Code and the New York State 
Income Tax Laws, the Town shall permit employee to establish a deferred compensation plan for 
said employee.

Page 9 of 9 
 
8.  The Town will provide a college and post -graduate incentive program for courses 
approved by the Town Board.  The Town will reimburse Cybulski the tuition cost on a grade related 
basis.  A grade of "A" will receive seventy five (75%) percent of the tuition cost.  A grade of "B" 
will receive fifty (50%) percent of the tuition cost.  A grade of "C" will receive twenty five (25%) 
percent of the tuition cost.  Payment will only be made upon submission of voucher and proof of 
grade. In addition to the above, the Town will reimburse Cybulski for 100 % costs related to 
certification(s) or license(s) subject to such certification or license is directly related to duties and 
responsibilities of his position as Deputy Wastewater Superintendent and written recommendation 
for approval by the Superintendent in an amount not to exceed $1500.00.  Notwithstanding the 
sentence immediately above, in the event that Cybulski terminates his employment with the Town 
within one year of receipt of said license or certification, Cybulski shall be required to refund and 
remit the costs related to said certification or license or in the alternative and at the discretion of the 
Town, the Town may deduct the costs from any accumulated vacation or sick leave compensation. 
 
 ARTICLE X 
 
 WAGES 
 
Cybulski shall receive the following annual salary: $107,500.00 for the period, January 1, 
2025 through December 31, 2025: (pro-rated in 2025). 
 
Cybulski’s base salary for each remaining year of this Agreement shall not be less than 
that of the preceding year. 
 
Effective and made applicable to January 1, 2026, Cybulski’s salary shall be increased 
annually based on the consumer price index for New York, Northern New Jersey, and Long Island 
limited and not to exceed 3.5%  or equal to the CSEA salary, Step and salary increase or 
enhancement, whichever is greater.  
 
IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the parties hereto by their duly authorized representatives have 
executed this Agreement the day and year stated above.

05.21.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-431 
 
REAPPOINTS A PROVISIONAL SENIOR WASTEWATER TREATMENT PLANT 
OPERATOR 2 
 
Councilwoman Merrifield offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilwoman Waski 
 
WHEREAS, Kevin Okula has been serving as a provisional appointment in the 
position of Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator 2 since January 1, 2025; and 
 
WHEREAS, on April 4, 2025  the Suffolk County Department of Civil Service  
established a certified List of Eligibles, list #2 5AF283, for the position of Senior 
Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator 2 , and there were less than three willing 
acceptors on the county list; and 
 
WHEREAS, Civil Service regulations allow for a second provisional appointment 
in such cases, and the department head has recommended that Mr. Okula be 
reappointed as a provisional Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator 2. 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED,  that pursuant to Civil Service 
regulations, this Town Board hereby reappoints Kevin Okula  to the position of 
provisional Senior Wastewater Treatment Plant Operator 2 effective today, May 21 , 
2025, at no change to his current salary or other level of benefits. 
 
RESOLVED, that Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device, and if needed, a certified copy of same 
can be obtained from the office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Denise Merrifield, Councilwoman 
SECONDER: Joann Waski, Councilwoman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

TB Resolution 2025-432 
 
APPOINTS A SEASONAL WATER TREATMENT PLANT OPERATOR IIB 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, there is a necessity for a seasonal Water Treatment Plant Operator 
to work in the Riverhead Water District during the summer season when demand is at a 
peak; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Water District Superintendent has made a recommendation to 
re-appoint Stephen Kelvas to this seasonal position as he holds the required license 
and is otherwise qualified for appointment. 
 
RESOLVED, that this Town Board hereby appoints Stephen Kelvas to the 
position of seasonal Water Treatment Plant Operator IIB at an hourly rate of $28.2444 
effective for the period of June 1, 2025 up to and including September 1, 2025. 
 
RESOLVED, all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of this 
resolution from the electronic storage device and if needed, a certified copy of same 
may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.

05.21.2025 ADOPTED 
 
 
TOWN OF RIVERHEAD 
 
TB Resolution 2025-436 
 
APPOINTS MEMBER TO THE TOWN OF RIVERHEAD HISPANIC DEVELOPMENT, 
EMPOWERMENT, AND EDUCATION COMMITTEE 
 
Councilwoman Waski offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Rothwell 
 
WHEREAS, the Town of Riverhead recognizes the importance of advancing 
economic development, empowerment, and education within its diverse community, and 
the need to ensure equitable opportunities for all residents; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town acknowledges the contributions and potential of the 
Hispanic community in Riverhead; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town seeks to accomplish these goals through the 
establishment of the Hispanic Development, Empowerment, and Education Committee 
(HDEEC) to focus on the advancement and empowerment of the Hispanic community in 
Riverhead; and 
 
WHEREAS, by Resolution #2025-169, adopted on February 4, 2025, the Town 
of Riverhead formally established the Hispanic Development, Empowerment, and 
Education Committee; and 
 
WHEREAS, Steven Ouzounian has expressed a desire and willingness to serve 
on the Hispanic Development, Empowerment, and Education Committee; and 
 
WHEREAS, the Town Board wishes to appoint Steven Ouzounian to the 
Hispanic Development, Empowerment, and Education Committee and, in order to 
effectuate an initial one-year term and create staggered terms among the members, 
desires that Steven Ouzounian's term be set to expire on December 31, 2025; 
 
NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the Riverhead Town Board hereby 
appoints Steven Ouzounian to the Town of Riverhead Hispanic Development, 
Empowerment, and Education Committee for a term to expire on December 31, 2025; 
and 
BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is  
hereby directed to forward a copy of this resolution to the Town Board Coordinator; and 
 
BE IT FURTHER RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and 
obtain a copy of this resolution from the electronic storage device, and if needed, a 
certified copy of same may be obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk. 
 
THE VOTE

RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Joann Waski, Councilwoman 
SECONDER: Kenneth Rothwell, Councilman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski

TB Resolution 2025-445 
 
APPROVES SPECIAL EVENT CHAPTER 255 APPLICATION FOR CHURCH OF THE 
HARVEST (EAST END CHURCH UNITY DAY) 
 
Councilman Rothwell offered the following resolution, 
which was seconded by Councilman Kern 
 
WHEREAS, on April 28, 2025 Church of the Harvest, submitted a Chapter 255 
Application for the purpose of conducting a Religious Service entitled East End Church 
Unity Day at Grangebel Park, Riverhead, New York, on September 13, 2025, between 
the hours of 2:00 p.m. to 8:00 p.m., with a rain date of September 20, 2025 and 
 
WHEREAS, the applicant has paid the requisite Chapter 255 Application fee of 
$175.00; and 
 
WHEREAS, A Comprehensive Liability Insurance Policy naming the Town of 
Riverhead, as an additional insured in the amount of $1,000,000 per occurrence             
and $2,000,000 general aggregate. Insurance coverage must include set-up and break-
down time and must list the name, date & location of the event under description of 
operations. If certificate of insurance is not received 15 days prior to the 
commencement of the event, the application shall be deemed incomplete and will 
be DENIED 
 
NOW THEREFORE BE IT RESOLVED, that the Town Board of the Town of 
Riverhead hereby has classified the action as a Type II under SEQRA NYCRR 617.5 C 
(21) and requiring no further environmental review; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that any tent installations, including the obtainment of any 
necessary tent permits, and any all electric shall comply with the applicable provisions 
of the Building and Fire Code of New York State, the National Electrical Code and 
National Fire Protection Association 102 (Tents & Membrane Structures); and be it 
further 
 
RESOLVED, that this approval is subject to the provisions of Riverhead Town 
Code Chapter 301-251 G (7) entitled “Signs” and any other section of the Riverhead 
Town Code that may pertain to this event; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Outdoor Safety Plan submitted with the applicant’s Chapter 
255 Application is subject to the review and approval of the Riverhead Fire Marshal; and 
be it further 
 
 RESOLVED, that should it be determined that police and or fire marshal 
personnel and vehicle usage become necessary for this event, then in that instance, 
Church of the Harvest agrees to pay the costs associated with same, which shall 
10.25
Packet Pg. 100
become due and payable upon delivery of an invoice to them for those additional costs; 
and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that all events taking place on Town property may be contingent 
upon the execution of a License Agreement with the Town of Riverhead within 7 days of 
the event and a fee of not less than $100.00; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that all events taking place on Town property that will have the sale 
or consumption of alcohol are contingent on NYS Liquor Authority approval for on -site 
consumption; and be it further, 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Supervisor is authorized to execute a license 
agreement for the use of Town property as well as with participating alcohol service 
vendors in a form to be approved by the Town Attorney’s Office; and be it further,  
 
RESOLVED, that the Chapter 255 Application of Church of the Harvest for the 
purpose of conducting A Religious Service entitled East End Church Unity Day on the 
aforesaid date and time, is hereby approved; and be it further 
 
RESOLVED, that the Town Clerk is hereby authorized to forward a copy of this 
resolution to Chief of Police, Edward Frost, Chief Fire Marshal, Andrew Smith, James 
Whelen LJwhelen@msn.com and be it further  
 
RESOLVED, that all Town Hall Departments may review and obtain a copy of 
this resolution from the electronic storage device and, if needed, a copy of same may be 
obtained from the Office of the Town Clerk.   
 
THE VOTE 
 
RESULT: ADOPTED [UNANIMOUS] 
MOVER: Kenneth Rothwell, Councilman 
SECONDER: Robert Kern, Councilman 
AYES: Hubbard, Rothwell, Kern, Merrifield, Waski
